#### SICK MAN MAINLINE EVENTS ####

turkfm.001 = { # The Sick Man of Europe
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.001.t
	desc = turkfm.001.d
	flavor = turkfm.001.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "turkfm_ottoman_intro"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ottoman.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered from GLOBAL
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_calculate_tension_effect = yes
		turkfm_awaken_jack_sparrow_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.001.a
		default_option = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_sick_man
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_decentralized_administration
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_separatist_tensions
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_imperial_aspiriations
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.100 # The Decaying Empire
				days = 30
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.200 # The Peoples of the Empire
				days = 90
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.900 # The Pirates of the Adriatic
				days = 150
			}
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.005 = { # Region Lost
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.005.t
	desc = turkfm.005.d
	flavor = turkfm.005.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "middleeast_battlefield_trenches"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ottoman.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_balkans
				turkfm_controls_balkans_trigger = no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_anatolia
				turkfm_controls_anatolia_trigger = no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_arabia
				turkfm_controls_arabia_trigger = no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_nile
				turkfm_controls_nile_trigger = no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_danubia
				turkfm_controls_danubia_trigger = no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_caucasus
				turkfm_controls_caucasus_trigger = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_balkans
				turkfm_controls_balkans_trigger = no
			}
			sr:region_balkans = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_sregion_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_anatolia
				turkfm_controls_anatolia_trigger = no
			}
			sr:region_anatolia = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_sregion_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_arabia
				turkfm_controls_arabia_trigger = no
			}
			sr:region_arabic = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_sregion_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_nile
				turkfm_controls_nile_trigger = no
			}
			sr:region_nile_basin = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_sregion_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_danubia
				turkfm_controls_danubia_trigger = no
			}
			sr:region_danubia = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_sregion_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_caucasus
				turkfm_controls_caucasus_trigger = no
			}
			sr:region_caucasus = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_sregion_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.005.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_region_lost_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_sregion_scope = sr:region_balkans
				}
				remove_variable = turkfm_controls_balkans
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_sregion_scope = sr:region_anatolia
				}
				remove_variable = turkfm_controls_anatolia
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_sregion_scope = sr:region_arabic
				}
				remove_variable = turkfm_controls_arabia
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_sregion_scope = sr:region_nile_basin
				}
				remove_variable = turkfm_controls_nile
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_sregion_scope = sr:region_danubia
				}
				remove_variable = turkfm_controls_danubia
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_sregion_scope = sr:region_nile_basin
				}
				remove_variable = turkfm_controls_nile
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_lost_region
				}
				remove_modifier = modifier_turkfm_lost_region
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_secured_region
			}
			remove_modifier = modifier_turkfm_secured_region
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_lost_region
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		turkfm_calculate_sick_man_effect = yes
	}

}

turkfm.006 = { # Region Secured
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.006.t
	desc = turkfm.006.d
	flavor = turkfm.006.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_military_parade"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ottoman.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_balkans
				}
				turkfm_controls_balkans_trigger = yes
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_anatolia
				}
				turkfm_controls_anatolia_trigger = yes
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_arabia
				}
				turkfm_controls_arabia_trigger = yes
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_nile
				}
				turkfm_controls_nile_trigger = yes
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_danubia
				}
				turkfm_controls_danubia_trigger = yes
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_caucasus
				}
				turkfm_controls_caucasus_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_balkans
				}
				turkfm_controls_balkans_trigger = yes
			}
			sr:region_balkans = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_sregion_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_anatolia
				}
				turkfm_controls_anatolia_trigger = yes
			}
			sr:region_anatolia = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_sregion_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_arabia
				}
				turkfm_controls_arabia_trigger = yes
			}
			sr:region_arabic = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_sregion_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_nile
				}
				turkfm_controls_nile_trigger = yes
			}
			sr:region_nile_basin = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_sregion_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_danubia
				}
				turkfm_controls_danubia_trigger = yes
			}
			sr:region_danubia = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_sregion_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_caucasus
				}
				turkfm_controls_caucasus_trigger = yes
			}
			sr:region_caucasus = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_sregion_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.006.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_region_secured_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_sregion_scope = sr:region_balkans
				}
				set_variable = turkfm_controls_balkans
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_sregion_scope = sr:region_anatolia
				}
				set_variable = turkfm_controls_anatolia
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_sregion_scope = sr:region_arabic
				}
				set_variable = turkfm_controls_arabia
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_sregion_scope = sr:region_nile_basin
				}
				set_variable = turkfm_controls_nile
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_sregion_scope = sr:region_danubia
				}
				set_variable = turkfm_controls_danubia
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_sregion_scope = sr:region_nile_basin
				}
				set_variable = turkfm_controls_nile
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_secured_region
				}
				remove_modifier = modifier_turkfm_secured_region
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_lost_region
			}
			remove_modifier = modifier_turkfm_lost_region
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_secured_region
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		turkfm_calculate_sick_man_effect = yes
	}
	
}

turkfm.007 = { # The Empire Shattered
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.007.t
	desc = turkfm.007.d
	flavor = turkfm.007.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_factory_closed"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm.008
	}
	
	
	immediate = {
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
			ruler = {
				save_scope_as = ottoman_ruler_scope
			}
		}
		random_primary_culture = {
			save_scope_as = primary_culture_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Rejoin the Empire
		name = turkfm.007.a
		default_option = yes
		c:TUR = {
			create_diplomatic_pact = {
				country = root
				type = tributary
			}
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = 50
		}
		c:TUR = {
			set_secret_goal = {
				country = root
				secret_goal = befriend
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 9
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Assert Your Destiny
		name = turkfm.007.b
		make_independent = yes
		add_loyalists = {
			culture = scope:primary_culture_scope
			value = large_radicals
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_sultanate_shattered
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		create_incident = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = 10
		}
		c:TUR = {
			set_secret_goal = {
				country = root
				secret_goal = conquer
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1 # Shouldn't really happen; if we get an economic dependence trigger, this will be expanded on
		}
	}

}

turkfm.008 = { # The Dead Man of Europe
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.008.t
	desc = turkfm.008.d
	flavor = turkfm.008.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_factory_closed"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by je_turkfm_sick_man_main
	}

	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.008.a
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {				
				is_subject = no
				any_subject_or_below = {
					NOT = { any_overlord_or_above = { NOT = { ROOT = this } } }
					NOT = {
						is_country_type = unrecognized
					}
				}
			}
			every_subject_or_below = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { any_overlord_or_above = { NOT = { ROOT = this } } }
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							is_country_type = unrecognized
						}
						is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
						is_subject_type = subject_type_dominion
						is_subject_type = subject_type_puppet
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = turkfm.007 # The Empire Shattered
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_type = unrecognized
	}

}

turkfm.101 = { # Edict of Gülhane
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.101.t
	desc = turkfm.101.d
	flavor = turkfm.101.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_adventure

	left_icon = scope:turkfm_ruler_scope
	
	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gbbf_backgrounds/gbbf_turkish_palace2.dds"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fez.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm_start_tanzimat_button
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ruler = {
			save_scope_as = turkfm_ruler_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.101.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_reorganizing_spirit
			years = 30
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_reform_completed_tt
			change_variable = {
				name = turkfm_tanzimat_completion_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_reform_completed_tt
			change_variable = {
				name = turkfm_tanzimat_completion_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				law_stance = {
					law = law_type:law_state_religion
					value > neutral
				}
				NOR = {
					law_stance = {
						law = law_type:law_landed_voting
						value > neutral
					}
					law_stance = {
						law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
						value > neutral
					}
					law_stance = {
						law = law_type:law_census_voting
						value > neutral
					}
					law_stance = {
						law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
						value > neutral
					}
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_influence_questioned
				months = long_modifier_time
				is_decaying = yes
			}
		}
		every_political_movement = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_political_movement_type = movement_religious_majority
					is_political_movement_type = movement_modernizer
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_declared_reforms
				years = 20
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_tanzimat_started
			}
		}
	}

}

turkfm.102 = { # The Men of the Tanzimat
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.102.t
	desc = turkfm.102.d
	flavor = turkfm.102.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_3char_selection

	left_icon = scope:turkfm_tanzimat_character_1
	center_icon = scope:turkfm_tanzimat_character_2
	right_icon = scope:turkfm_tanzimat_character_3
	
	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gbbf_backgrounds/gbbf_turkish_palace1.dds"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = turkfm_tanzimat_men_happened
		}
		has_global_variable = turkfm_tanzimat_started
		var:turkfm_tanzimat_completion_var > 0
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = turkfm_tanzimat_men_happened
		if = {
			limit = {
				ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
					leader = {
						has_template = template_turkfm_reshid_mustafa
					}
				}
			}
			ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
				leader = {
					save_scope_as = turkfm_tanzimat_character_1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_character = {
				template = template_turkfm_reshid_mustafa
				on_created = {
					place_character_in_void = 12
				}
			}
			random_character_in_void = {
				limit = {
					has_template = template_turkfm_reshid_mustafa
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_tanzimat_character_1
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			template = template_turkfm_ali_mehmed
			on_created = {
				place_character_in_void = 12
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_turkfm_ali_mehmed
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tanzimat_character_2
		}
		create_character = {
			template = template_turkfm_fuad_mehmed
			on_created = {
				place_character_in_void = 12
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_turkfm_fuad_mehmed
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tanzimat_character_3
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.102.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_reorganizing_spirit
			months = very_long_modifier_time
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
					leader = scope:turkfm_tanzimat_character_1
				}
			}
			scope:turkfm_tanzimat_character_1 = {
				add_trait = trait_turkfm_master_bureaucrat
			}
			scope:turkfm_tanzimat_character_2 = {
				add_character_role = agitator
				hidden_effect = {
					free_character_from_void = yes
				}
			}
			scope:turkfm_tanzimat_character_3 = {
				add_character_role = agitator
				hidden_effect = {
					free_character_from_void = yes
				}
			}

		}
		else = {
			scope:turkfm_tanzimat_character_1 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						empty_agitator_slots > 0
					}
					add_character_role = agitator
					hidden_effect = {
						free_character_from_void = yes
					}
				}
			}
			scope:turkfm_tanzimat_character_2 = {
				add_character_role = agitator
				hidden_effect = {
					free_character_from_void = yes
				}
			}
			scope:turkfm_tanzimat_character_3 = {
				add_character_role = agitator
				hidden_effect = {
					free_character_from_void = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

turkfm.201 = { # The Rise of Nationalism
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.200.t
	desc = turkfm.200.d
	flavor = turkfm.200.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "middleeast_middleclass_cafe"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/waving_flag.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = turkfm_nationalism_wave_happened
		}
		OR = {
			has_technology_researched = nationalism
			any_country = {
				is_subject_of = root
				capital = {
					region = sr:region_balkans
					region = sr:region_danubia
				}
				has_technology_researched = nationalism
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = turkfm_nationalism_wave_happened
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_technology_researched = nationalism
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_nationalism_scope
		}
		else = {
			random_country = {
				limit =	{
					is_subject_of = root
					capital = {
						region = sr:region_balkans
						region = sr:region_danubia
					}
					has_technology_researched = nationalism
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_nationalism_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.201.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = turkfm_nationalism_tension_tt
	}

}

turkfm.204 = { # Adds je_turkfm_separatism_main
	type = country_event
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_global_variable = turkfm_separatism_complete
			has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_separatism_main
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			region = sr:region_balkans
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_tension_started
			}
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_turkfm_separatism_main
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_turkfm_separatism_main
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.200 # The Peoples of the Empire
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
				s:STATE_CROATIA.region_state:TUR = {

					save_scope_as = turkfm_riot_state_scope
				}
			}

				trigger = {
					owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SLAVONIA
				}
				s:STATE_SLAVONIA.region_state:TUR = {
					save_scope_as = turkfm_riot_state_scope
				}
			}
		}
		scope:turkfm_riot_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_race_riots
		}
		change_global_variable = {
			name = turkfm_riot_counter_var
			add = 1
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = turkfm_riot_current_tally_var
			add = 1
		}
		if = {

				name = turkfm_riot_var
				value = 100

				post_notification = notification_turkfm_race_riots
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_race_riots_worsen
			}
		}
		turkfm_update_riot_variables_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.205.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = turkfm.205.tt
		show_as_tooltip = {
			scope:turkfm_riot_state_scope = {
				add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_race_riots
			}
		}
	}

}

turkfm.206 = { # Balkan Country Rebellion
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_rebellion_scope
	
	title = turkfm.206.t
	desc = turkfm.206.d
	flavor = turkfm.206.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_agitator_speaking"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/waving_flag.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			global_var:turkfm_separatism_phase_var ?= 5 # Crisis
		}
		var:turkfm_riot_var >= 200
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		months = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_create_rebellion_effect = yes
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_rebellion_tag_tracker
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_rebellion_scope
			remove_variable = turkfm_rebellion_tag_tracker
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = turkfm_riot_var
			value = 100
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_relevance = root
			}
			create_bidirectional_truce = {
				country = scope:turkfm_rebellion_scope
				months = 60
			}
		}
		create_bidirectional_truce = {
			country = scope:turkfm_rebellion_scope
			months = 60
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Assert Our Dominion
		name = turkfm.206.a
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			end_truce = scope:turkfm_rebellion_scope
		}
		scope:turkfm_rebellion_scope = {
			make_independent = yes
		}
		create_diplomatic_play = {
			name = turkfm_balkan_rebellion
			target_country = scope:turkfm_rebellion_scope
			type = dp_secession
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_diplomatic_play = {
				limit = {
					c:TUR = {
						is_diplomatic_play_initiator = yes
					}
					scope:turkfm_rebellion_scope = {
						is_diplomatic_play_target = yes
					}
				}
				add_diplomatic_play_war_support = { target = scope:turkfm_rebellion_scope value = 100 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_revolt_seccession
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Let Them Go
		name = turkfm.206.b
		create_diplomatic_pact = {
			country = scope:turkfm_rebellion_scope
			type = protectorate
		}
		add_radicals = {
			culture = cu:turkish
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_caved_to_separatists
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_revolt_protectorate
			}
		}
	}

}

			}
			post_notification = notification_turkfm_riot_suppressed
		}
	}

turkfm.208 = { # Region Lost
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.208.t
	desc = turkfm.208.d
	flavor = turkfm.208.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "middleeast_battlefield_trenches"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = turkfm_lost_region_var
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_balkans
				turkfm_controls_balkans_trigger = no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_anatolia
				turkfm_controls_anatolia_trigger = no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_arabia
				turkfm_controls_arabia_trigger = no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_nile
				turkfm_controls_nile_trigger = no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_danubia
				turkfm_controls_danubia_trigger = no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_caucasus
				turkfm_controls_caucasus_trigger = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_balkans
				turkfm_controls_balkans_trigger = no
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = turkfm_lost_region_var
				value = 1 # Balkans
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_anatolia
				turkfm_controls_anatolia_trigger = no
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = turkfm_lost_region_var
				value = 2 # Anatolia
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_arabia
				turkfm_controls_arabia_trigger = no
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = turkfm_lost_region_var
				value = 3 # Arabia
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_nile
				turkfm_controls_nile_trigger = no
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = turkfm_lost_region_var
				value = 4 # Nile
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_danubia
				turkfm_controls_danubia_trigger = no
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = turkfm_lost_region_var
				value = 5 # Danubia
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_controls_caucasus
				turkfm_controls_caucasus_trigger = no
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = turkfm_lost_region_var
				value = 6 # Caucasus
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.208.a
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_secured_region
			}
			remove_modifier = modifier_turkfm_secured_region
		}
		hidden_effect = {	
			remove_modifier = modifier_turkfm_lost_region
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_lost_region
			months = normal_modifier_time
			is_decaying = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:turkfm_lost_region_var = 1
			}
			remove_variable = turkfm_controls_balkans
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:turkfm_lost_region_var = 2
			}
			remove_variable = turkfm_controls_anatolia
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:turkfm_lost_region_var = 3
			}
			remove_variable = turkfm_controls_arabia
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:turkfm_lost_region_var = 4
			}
			remove_variable = turkfm_controls_nile
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:turkfm_lost_region_var = 5
			}
			remove_variable = turkfm_controls_danubia
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:turkfm_lost_region_var = 6
			}
			remove_variable = turkfm_controls_caucasus
		}
		remove_variable = turkfm_lost_region_var
	}

}

turkfm.209 = { # Region Secured
	type = country_event
	placement = root

	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = turkfm_gained_region_var
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_balkans
				}
				turkfm_controls_balkans_trigger = yes
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_anatolia
				}
				turkfm_controls_anatolia_trigger = yes
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_arabia
				}
				turkfm_controls_arabia_trigger = yes
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {

				}
				turkfm_controls_nile_trigger = yes
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_danubia
				}
				turkfm_controls_danubia_trigger = yes
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_controls_caucasus
				}
				turkfm_controls_caucasus_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

					has_variable = turkfm_controls_balkans

				NOT = {

				}
				turkfm_controls_arabia_trigger = yes
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = turkfm_gained_region_var
				value = 3 # Arabia
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {

				turkfm_controls_nile_trigger = yes
			}
			set_variable = {

			}
			set_variable = {

			}
		}

turkfm.210 = { # Extortionate Taxation in State
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.210.t
	desc = turkfm.210.d
	flavor = turkfm.210.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_russian_serfs"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_neutral_events_trigger = yes
		institution_investment_level = {
			institution = institution_millet_system 
			value >= 3
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_overtaxed
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_tax_break_given
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
		}
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Maintain Taxation
		name = turkfm.210.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_overtaxed
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_overtaxed
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Reduce Taxation
		name = turkfm.210.b
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_tax_break_given
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				pop_type = aristocrats
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_tax_break
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_deescalation_effect = yes
	}
	
}

turkfm.214 = { # Food Shortages in State
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.214.t
	desc = turkfm.214.d
	flavor = turkfm.214.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "asia_dead_cattle_poor_harvest"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_neutral_events_trigger = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			state_region = {
				OR = {
					has_harvest_condition = drought
					has_harvest_condition = flood
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_variable = turkfm_food_shortage_var
			}
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
				state_region = {
					OR = {
						has_harvest_condition = drought
						has_harvest_condition = flood
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_food_shortage_var
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = turkfm_food_shortage_var
				years = 5
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.214.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_sent_relief_column
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_relief_provided
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.214.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = large_radicals
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_relief_denied
			}
		}
	}

}

turkfm.215 = { # Peasants March in State
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.215.t
	desc = turkfm.215.d
	flavor = turkfm.215.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_cops_march"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_protest.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_neutral_events_trigger = yes
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # End the Marches
		name = turkfm.215.a
		default_option = yes
		show_as_unavailable = {
			always = yes
		}
		highlighted_option = yes
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_law = law_type:law_right_of_assembly
				has_law = law_type:law_protected_speech
			}
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata = poor
				value = medium_radicals
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_supressed_marches
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Tolerate the Marches
		name = turkfm.215.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				strata = poor
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_tolerated_dissent
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_deescalation_effect = yes
	}

}

turkfm.216 = { # Local Bey Exceeds Authority
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.216.t
	desc = turkfm.216.d
	flavor = turkfm.216.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_cops_march"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_protest.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_neutral_events_trigger = yes
		institution_investment_level = {
			institution = institution_millet_system 
			value > 1
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_domineering_bey
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_recalled_bey
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_domineering_bey
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Sanction his actions
		name = turkfm.216.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_domineering_bey
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_recalled_bey
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_small_escalation_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Recall the Bey
		name = turkfm.216.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_recalled_bey
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				pop_type = aristocrats
				value = medium_radicals
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_domineering_bey
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_deescalation_effect = yes
	}
	

}

turkfm.217 = { # Church Services Disrupted
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.217.t
	desc = turkfm.217.d
	flavor = turkfm.217.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "southamerica_christianity"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_orthodox.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_neutral_events_trigger = yes
		institution_investment_level = {
			institution = institution_millet_system 
			value < 5
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_churches_disrupted
			}
			any_scope_pop = {
				has_pop_religion = orthodox
			}
			any_scope_pop = {
				has_pop_religion = sunni
			}
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 4
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_churches_disrupted
				}
				any_scope_pop = {
					has_pop_religion = orthodox
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Stick up for the Churches
		name = turkfm.217.a
		default_option = yes
		ig:ig_devout = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_protected_churches
				months = normal_modifier_time
				is_decaying = yes
			}
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = medium_radicals
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:sunni
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_small_deescalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_protected_churches
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # lol who cares
		name = turkfm.217.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_churches_disrupted
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = large_radicals
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_churches_disrupted
			}
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.218 = { # Villages Request Schools
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.218.t
	desc = turkfm.218.d
	flavor = turkfm.218.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "africa_public_protest"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_neutral_events_trigger = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_funding_schools
				has_variable = turkfm_schools_requested
			}
			any_scope_pop = {
				has_pop_religion = orthodox
				pop_acceptance < acceptance_status_4
				wealth < 20
				literacy_rate < 0.33
			}
			any_scope_pop = {
				is_pop_type = academics
			}
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 10
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_funding_schools
					has_variable = turkfm_schools_requested
				}
				any_scope_pop = {
					has_pop_religion = orthodox
					pop_acceptance < acceptance_status_4
					wealth < 20
					literacy_rate < 0.33
				}
				any_scope_pop = {
					is_pop_type = academics
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
			set_variable = {
				name = turkfm_schools_requested
				years = 20
			}
			random_scope_pop = {
				limit = {
					has_pop_religion = orthodox
					pop_acceptance < acceptance_status_4
					wealth < 20
					literacy_rate < 0.33
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_culture_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Deny Funding
		name = turkfm.218.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				pop_type = academics
				value = medium_radicals
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_schools_denied
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Grant Funding
		name = turkfm.218.b
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_funding_schools
			months = normal_modifier_time
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_medium
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_state_schools
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				pop_type = aristocrats
				value = medium_radicals
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_schools_approved
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_small_deescalation_effect = yes
	}

}

turkfm.219 = { # Revivalist Publications
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.219.t
	desc = turkfm.219.d
	flavor = turkfm.219.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "ep1_printing_press"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_neutral_events_trigger = yes
		turkfm_can_escalate_tension_trigger = yes
		has_technology_researched = mass_communication
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_nationalist_newspaper
			}
			any_scope_pop = {
				has_pop_religion = orthodox
				pop_acceptance < acceptance_status_4
				literacy_rate > 0.33
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_nationalist_newspaper
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
			random_scope_pop = {
				limit = {
					has_pop_religion = orthodox
					pop_acceptance < acceptance_status_4
					literacy_rate > 0.33
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_culture_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Shut it Down
		name = turkfm.219.a
		default_option = yes
		show_as_unavailable = {
			always = yes
		}
		highlighted_option = yes
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_law = law_type:law_right_of_assembly
				has_law = law_type:law_protected_speech
			}
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_nationalist_newspaper
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = large_radicals
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_censored_paper
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_newspaper_censored
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_large_escalation_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Tolerate It
		name = turkfm.219.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_nationalist_newspaper
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = large_radicals
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_newspaper_ignored
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
	}

}

#### MILLET UNREST EVENTS ####

turkfm.220 = { # Storefronts Ransacked
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.220.t
	desc = turkfm.220.d
	flavor = turkfm.220.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_vandalized_storefront"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_unrest_events_trigger = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_stores_ransacked
			}
			any_scope_pop = {
				has_pop_religion = orthodox
				pop_acceptance < acceptance_status_4
			}
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_stores_ransacked
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
			random_scope_pop = {
				limit = {
					has_pop_religion = orthodox
					pop_acceptance < acceptance_status_4
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_culture_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Take No Action
		name = turkfm.220.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_stores_ransacked
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				months = normal_modifier_time
				multiplier = -2
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_stores_ransacked
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Provide Reparations
		name = turkfm.220.b
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_providing_reparations
			months = short_modifier_time
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_medium
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_stores_ransacked
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				value = medium_radicals
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				culture = cu:turkish
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_stores_ransacked
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_small_escalation_effect = yes
	}

}

turkfm.221 = { # Minority Rejects Classification
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.221.t
	desc = turkfm.221.d
	flavor = turkfm.221.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "africa_public_protest"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_protest.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_unrest_events_trigger = yes
		institution_investment_level = {
			institution = institution_millet_system 
			value >= 3
		}
		NOR = {
			has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_enforced_millets
			has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_millets_eroding
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			any_scope_pop = {
				has_pop_religion = orthodox
				NOR = {
					has_pop_culture = greek
					has_pop_culture = rhomaios
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 20
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
			}
			random_scope_pop = {
				limit = {
					has_pop_religion = orthodox
					NOR = {
						has_pop_culture = greek
						has_pop_culture = rhomaios
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_culture_scope
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = { # Enforce the Classification
		name = turkfm.221.a
		default_option = yes
		add_radicals = {
			religion = rel:orthodox
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		add_loyalists = {
			pop_type = clergymen
			value = large_radicals
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_enforced_millets
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_millets_enforced
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Relent on Classifications
		name = turkfm.221.b
		add_loyalists = {
			religion = rel:orthodox
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		add_radicals = {
			religion = rel:muslim
			value = small_radicals
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_millets_eroding

turkfm.223 = { # Crowds Gather in City Hub
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.223.t
	desc = turkfm.223.d
	flavor = turkfm.223.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_political_extremism"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_protest.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_unrest_events_trigger = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			any_scope_pop = {
				has_pop_religion = orthodox
				pop_radical_fraction = {
					value > 0.20
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
				any_scope_pop = {
					has_pop_religion = orthodox
					pop_radical_fraction = {
						value > 0.20
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
			random_scope_pop = {
				limit = {
					has_pop_religion = orthodox
					pop_radical_fraction = {
						value > 0.20
					}
				}
				culture = {
					save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Disperse the Crowds
		name = turkfm.223.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_crowds_dispersed
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Give them a Space
		name = turkfm.223.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				culture = cu:turkish
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_cultural_protests
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		turkfm_add_small_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_crowds_tolerated
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Beat Them Down
		name = turkfm.223.c
		show_as_unavailable = {
			always = yes
		}
		highlighted_option = yes
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_law = law_type:law_militarized_police
				has_law = law_type:law_outlawed_dissent
			}
		}
		add_radicals = {
			culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
			value = large_radicals
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				percent = 0.02
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_cultural_supression
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				months = normal_modifier_time
				multiplier = -2
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_large_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_crowds_beaten
			}
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.224 = { # Language Bans in State
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.224.t
	desc = turkfm.224.d
	flavor = turkfm.224.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = turkfm_language_ban_considered
		}
		turkfm_unrest_events_trigger = yes
		institution_investment_level = {
			institution = institution_millet_system 
			value <= 3
		}
		NOR = {
			has_law = law_type:law_protected_speech
			has_law = law_type:law_guaranteed_liberties
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			any_scope_pop = {
				OR = {
					has_pop_religion = orthodox
					has_pop_religion = jewish
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = turkfm_language_ban_considered
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
				any_scope_pop = {
					OR = {
						has_pop_religion = orthodox
						has_pop_religion = jewish
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ignore the Ban
		name = turkfm.224.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_languages_banned
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = medium_radicals
				religion = rel:orthodox
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = medium_radicals
				religion = rel:jewish
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_large_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_local_language_ban
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Rescind the Ban
		name = turkfm.224.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_languages_protected
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				value = medium_radicals
				religion = rel:orthodox
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				value = medium_radicals
				religion = rel:jewish
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_large_deescalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_languages_protected
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Extend the Ban Empire-wide
		name = turkfm.224.c
		show_as_unavailable = {
			always = yes
		}
		highlighted_option = yes
		trigger = {
			institution_investment_level = {
				institution = institution_millet_system 
				value >= 3
			}
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_languages_banned
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = medium_radicals
				religion = rel:orthodox
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = medium_radicals
				religion = rel:ewish
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_very_large_escalation_effect = yes
		change_infamy = 10
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_total_language_ban
			}
		}
	}
		
}

turkfm.225 = { # Gun-Runners Intercepted (Greek)
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.225.t
	desc = turkfm.225.d
	flavor = turkfm.225.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "rp1_social_banditry"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_unrest_events_trigger = yes
		any_country = {
			has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_supporting_gunrunners
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 4
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					owns_entire_state_region = STATE_THESSALIA
				}
				s:STATE_THESSALIA = {
					random_scope_state = {
						save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					owns_entire_state_region = STATE_MACEDONIA
				}
				s:STATE_MACEDONIA = {
					random_scope_state = {
						save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SKOPIA
				}
				s:STATE_SKOPIA = {
					random_scope_state = {
						save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					owns_entire_state_region = STATE_CRETE
				}
				s:STATE_CRETE = {
					random_scope_state = {
						save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					owns_entire_state_region = STATE_AYDIN
				}
				s:STATE_AYDIN = {
					random_scope_state = {
						save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					owns_entire_state_region = STATE_CYPRUS
				}
				s:STATE_CYPRUS = {
					random_scope_state = {
						save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
					}
				}
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_supporting_gunrunners
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_country_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Press the Issue
		name = turkfm.225.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_arrested_gunrunners
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			set_variable = turkfm_gunrunners_var
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_country_scope = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.311 # Gun-Runners Arrested
			}
			create_incident = {
				country = root
				value = 5
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_deescalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_greek_gunrunners_arrested
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Grant Amnesty
		name = turkfm.225.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_gunrunner_amnesty
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				pop_type = officers
				value = medium_radicals
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				pop_type = soldiers
				value = small_radicals
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_greek_gunrunners_released
			}
		}
	}

}

turkfm.228 = { # Villagers Displaced in State
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.228.t
	desc = turkfm.228.d
	flavor = turkfm.228.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "southamerica_war_civilians"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_unrest_events_trigger = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			state_region = {
				is_homeland = cu:turkish
			}
			NOT = {
				has_variable = turkfm_settler_conflict_var
			}
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 5
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
				state_region = {
					is_homeland = cu:turkish
				}
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_settler_conflict_var
				}
			}
			set_variable = turkfm_settler_conflict_var
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
			random_scope_pop = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_pop_religion = orthodox
						has_pop_religion = jewish
					}
				}
				culture = {
					save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ignore the Issue
		name = turkfm.228.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = {
				culture = cu:turkish
				months = long_modifier_time
				multiplier = 1
			}
			add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				months = long_modifier_time
				multiplier = -2
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				value = large_radicals
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_ignored_displacement
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Restrict Settlements
		name = turkfm.228.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = {
				culture = cu:turkish
				months = long_modifier_time
				multiplier = 1
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				culture = cu:turkish
				value = small_radicals
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_deescalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_restricted_displacement
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Support Settlements
		name = turkfm.228.c
		show_as_unavailable = { always = yes }
		highlighted_option = yes
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_law = law_type:law_colonial_resettlement
				has_law = law_type:law_colonial_exploitation
			}
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = {
				culture = cu:turkish
				months = long_modifier_time
				multiplier = 2
			}
			add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				months = long_modifier_time
				multiplier = -4
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				value = very_large_radicals
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_minorities_displaced
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_very_large_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_supported_displacement
			}
		}
	}

}

turkfm.229 = { # Brigands Cross the Border
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.229.t
	desc = turkfm.229.d
	flavor = turkfm.229.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_cops_march"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_unrest_events_trigger = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_brigandage
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			is_adjacent_to_country = root
			has_journal_entry = je_balkfm_brigandage
			relations:root < relations_threshold:amicable
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_brigandage_reparations_positive
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_brigandage
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_adjacent_to_country = root
				has_journal_entry = je_balkfm_brigandage
				relations:root < relations_threshold:amicable
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_country_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Seek Redress
		name = turkfm.229.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_brigandage
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			set_variable = turkfm_brigandage_event_var
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_country_scope = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.310 # Brigands Raid Turkish Lands
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_small_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_brigandage_dispute
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Extend an Olive Branch
		name = turkfm.229.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_brigandage
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:turkfm_tension_country_scope
			value = 15
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_country_scope = {
			post_notification = notification_turkfm_brigandage_ignored
		}
		turkfm_add_small_deescalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
					NOT = {
						scope:turkfm_tension_country_scope = this
					}
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_brigandage_conciliation
			}
		}
	}

}

turkfm.230 = { # Churches Burned in State
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.230.t
	desc = turkfm.230.d
	flavor = turkfm.230.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_vandalized_storefront"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_hostility_events_trigger = yes
		NOT = {
			any_state = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_churches_burned
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_churches_burned
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # They Can Deal With It
		name = turkfm.230.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = medium_radicals
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_churches_burned
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_churches_burned
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Pay Them Back
		name = turkfm.230.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = small_radicals
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_churches_burned
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_rebuilding_churches
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			owner = {
				add_treasury = -20000
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_small_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_church_reparations
			}
		}
	}

}

turkfm.234 = { # Blood Libel
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.234.t
	desc = turkfm.234.d
	flavor = turkfm.234.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_agitator_speaking"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_hostility_events_trigger = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			any_scope_pop = {
				OR = {
					has_pop_religion = orthodox
					has_pop_religion = oriental_orthodox
					has_pop_religion = jewish
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 2
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
				any_scope_pop = {
					OR = {
						has_pop_religion = orthodox
						has_pop_religion = oriental_orthodox
						has_pop_religion = jewish
					}
					pop_acceptance < 60
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
			random_scope_pop = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_pop_religion = orthodox
						has_pop_religion = oriental_orthodox
						has_pop_religion = jewish
					}
					pop_acceptance < 60
				}
				religion = {
					save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_religion_scope
				}
				culture = {
					save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Not our problem
		name = turkfm.234.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = {

				months = short_modifier_time

			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = scope:turkfm_tension_religion_scope
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_large_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
				}
				post_notification = notification_turkfm_blood_libel_ignored
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Put a lid on their antics
		name = turkfm.234.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				months = short_modifier_time
				multiplier = -1
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				religion = scope:turkfm_tension_religion_scope
				value = small_radicals
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {

			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Launch an Expedition
		name = turkfm.236.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				value = large_radicals
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				pop_type = officers
				value = medium_radicals
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				pop_type = soldiers
				value = medium_radicals
			}
			add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				months = short_modifier_time
				multiplier = -2
			}
			state_region = {
				add_devastation = 5
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_large_deescalation_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Limit Patrols
		name = turkfm.236.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_insecure_highways
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				culture = cu:turkish
				value = large_radicals
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				pop_type = aristocrats
				value = medium_radicals
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				pop_type = officers
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_large_escalation_effect = yes
	}

}

turkfm.237 = { # Muslim Militia Organizes in State
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.237.t
	desc = turkfm.237.d
	flavor = turkfm.237.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "rp1_social_banditry"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_protest.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_hostility_events_trigger = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			state_in_balkans = yes
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_muslim_militia
				has_variable = turkfm_denied_militia_var
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_muslim_militia
					has_variable = turkfm_denied_militia_var
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Encourage this effort
		name = turkfm.237.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_muslim_militia
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				religion = rel:sunni
				value = large_radicals
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = large_radicals
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:oriental_orthodox
				value = large_radicals
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:jewish
				value = large_radicals
			}
		}
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				law_stance = {
					law = law_type:law_state_religion
					value > 0
				}
				law_stance = {
					law = law_type:law_professional_army
					value <= 0
				}
				law_stance = {
					law = law_type:law_mass_conscription
					value <= 0
				}
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_approves_militia
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_approves_militia
				months = long_modifier_time
				is_decaying = yes
			}
		}
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					law_stance = {
						law = law_type:law_professional_army
						value > 0
					}
					law_stance = {
						law = law_type:law_mass_conscription
						value > 0
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_disapproves_militia
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_disapproves_militia
				months = long_modifier_time
				is_decaying = yes
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_large_escalation_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Discourage this effort
		name = turkfm.237.b
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			set_variable = {
				name = turkfm_denied_militia_var
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:sunni
				value = large_radicals
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_large_deescalation_effect = yes
	}

}

	}

		turkfm_hostility_events_trigger = yes

			state_in_balkans = yes

				has_variable = turkfm_crowd_massacre_var
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_in_balkans = yes

				}
			}
			set_variable = turkfm_crowd_massacre_var

		}
	}

				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				value = large_radicals
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_civilians_killed
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				months = normal_modifier_time
				multiplier = -1
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_deescalation_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Encourage the Garrison

			kill_population_in_state = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				value = 1000
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				value = very_large_radicals
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				religion = rel:orthodox
				value = large_radicals
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_civilians_massacred
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			add_culture_standard_of_living_modifier = {
				culture = scope:turkfm_tension_culture_scope
				months = normal_modifier_time
				multiplier = -2
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_large_escalation_effect = yes
	}

turkfm.242 = { # Great Power Mediates Local Conflict
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.242.t
	desc = turkfm.242.d
	flavor = turkfm.242.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "ep1_power_blocs"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm.312
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_tension_third_party_var
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_country_scope
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_intervention_var
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_tension_state_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Accept the Assist
		name = turkfm.242.a
		default_option = yes
		turkfm_add_large_deescalation_effect = yes
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:turkfm_tension_country_scope
			value = 15
		}
		create_diplomatic_catalyst = {
			type = catalyst_relations_level_increased
			target = scope:turkfm_tension_country_scope
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_tensions_defused
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_country_scope = {
			post_notification = notification_turkfm_tensions_defused
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Reject the Assist
		name = turkfm.242.b
		turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:turkfm_tension_country_scope
			value = -25
		}
		create_diplomatic_catalyst = {
			type = catalyst_relations_level_decreased
			target = scope:turkfm_tension_country_scope
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_country_scope = {
			post_notification = notification_turkfm_tensions_ignored
		}
		
	}
	
	after = {
		scope:turkfm_tension_country_scope = {
			remove_variable = turkfm_tension_third_party_var
		}
		scope:turkfm_tension_state_scope = {
			remove_variable = turkfm_intervention_var
		}
	}

}

			}			
		}

			}
			2 = {

			}
		}
	}

		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_race_riots
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_government_administration
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_riot_state_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Where are the cops?
		name = turkfm.251.a
		default_option = yes
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				scope:turkfm_riot_state_scope = {
					add_radicals_in_state = {
						value = medium_radicals
					}				
				}
			}
			1 = {
				turkfm_add_medium_deescalation_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Deploy the Garrison
		name = turkfm.251.b
		trigger = {
			scope:turkfm_riot_state_scope = {
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_garrison_disarmed
				}
			}
		}
		show_as_unavailable = {
			always = yes
		}
		highlighted_option = yes
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				scope:turkfm_riot_state_scope = {
					add_loyalists_in_state = {
						value = small_radicals
					}				
				}
			}
			1 = {
				turkfm_add_small_escalation_effect = yes
			}
		}
		add_modifier = { 
			name = modifier_turkfm_deployed_garrison
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_small
			months = short_modifier_time
		}
	}
}

turkfm.254 = { # Armed Forces Requests Intervention
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.254.t
	desc = turkfm.254.d
	flavor = turkfm.254.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_before_the_battle"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_military.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_hostility_events_trigger = yes
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_intervention_denied
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_intervention_granted
			}
			ig_approval > 5
			leader = {
				NOR = {
					has_ideology = ideology:ideology_pacifist
					has_ideology = ideology:ideology_radical
					has_ideology = ideology:ideology_anarchist
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_separatism_riots
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_race_riots
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_riot_state_scope
		}
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			save_scope_as = turkfm_riot_ig_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Grant the Order
		name = turkfm.254.a
		default_option = yes
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_intervention_granted
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		scope:turkfm_riot_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_military_intervention
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
		}
		add_radicals = {
			religion = rel:orthodox
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		random_list = {
			2 = {
				turkfm_add_small_deescalation_effect = yes
			}
			1 = {
				turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Have them pack up and leave
		name = turkfm.254.b
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_intervention_denied
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		add_radicals = {
			pop_type = officers
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		turkfm_add_small_escalation_effect = yes
	}

}
