turkfm.257 = { # Rioting Worsens in State
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:t
	
	title = turkfm.257.t
	desc = turkfm.257.d
	flavor = turkfm.257.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_springtime_of_nations"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		turkfm_hostility_events_trigger = yes
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_separatism_riots
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_tension_cooldown_effect = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_race_riots
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_riot_state_scope
			set_variable = turkfm_riot_state_var
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Leave it to local officers
		name = turkfm.257.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = { 
			name = modifier_turkfm_deployed_garrison
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			months = short_modifier_time
		}
		scope:turkfm_riot_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_mass_arrests
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_scope_pop = {
						has_pop_religion = orthodox
					}
				}
				add_radicals_in_state = {
					religion = rel:orthodox
					value = large_radicals
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_scope_pop = {
						has_pop_religion = oriental_orthodox
					}
				}
				add_radicals_in_state = {
					religion = rel:oriental_orthodox
					value = large_radicals
				}
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { 
			random_list = {
				50 = { 
					trigger_event = {
						id = turkfm.258 # Massacre in State
						days = 15
					}
				}
				50 = { 
					trigger_event = {
						id = turkfm.259 # Crowds Dispersed in State
						days = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Let them protest
		name = turkfm.257.b
		scope:mob_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_massive_riots
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_scope_pop = {
						has_pop_religion = orthodox
					}
				}
				add_radicals_in_state = {
					religion = rel:orthodox
					value = medium_radicals
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_scope_pop = {
						has_pop_religion = oriental_orthodox
					}
				}
				add_radicals_in_state = {
					religion = rel:oriental_orthodox
					value = medium_radicals
				}
			}
			remove_variable = turkfm_riot_state_var
		}
		add_radicals = {
			religion = rel:sunni
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		turkfm_add_large_escalation_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Send the military
		name = turkfm.257.c
		add_modifier = { 
			name = modifier_turkfm_deployed_army
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_medium
			months = short_modifier_time
		}
		scope:mob_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_military_intervention
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_scope_pop = {
						has_pop_religion = orthodox
					}
				}
				add_radicals_in_state = {
					religion = rel:orthodox
					value = very_large_radicals
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_scope_pop = {
						has_pop_religion = oriental_orthodox
					}
				}
				add_radicals_in_state = {
					religion = rel:oriental_orthodox
					value = very_large_radicals
				}
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				religion = rel:sunni
				value = very_large_radicals
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_medium_deescalation_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { 
			random_list = {
				80 = { 
					trigger_event = {
						id = turkfm.258 # Massacre in State
						days = 15
					}
				}
				20 = { 
					trigger_event = {
						id = turkfm.259 # Crowds Dispersed in State
						days = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

					}
				}

					religion = rel:oriental_orthodox
					value = medium_radicals
				}
			}

turkfm.290 = { # Hellenes Stage Revolt in State
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.290.t
	desc = turkfm.290.d
	flavor = turkfm.290.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_springtime_of_nations"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			global_var:turkfm_separatism_phase_var ?= 4 # Deconfliction
			has_global_variable = turkfm_greek_rebellion_cooldown
		}
		any_country = {
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:greek
			has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_supporting_gunrunners
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_ALBANIA
				s:STATE_ALBANIA = {
					any_scope_state = {
						OR = {
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:greek
								value >= 0.50
							}
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:rhomaios
								value >= 0.50
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_MACEDONIA
				s:STATE_MACEDONIA = {
					any_scope_state = {
						OR = {
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:greek
								value >= 0.50
							}
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:rhomaios
								value >= 0.50
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SKOPIA
				s:STATE_SKOPIA = {
					any_scope_state = {
						OR = {
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:greek
								value >= 0.50
							}
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:rhomaios
								value >= 0.50
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_CYPRUS
				s:STATE_CYPRUS = {
					any_scope_state = {
						OR = {
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:greek
								value >= 0.50
							}
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:rhomaios
								value >= 0.50
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_CRETE
				s:STATE_CRETE = {
					any_scope_state = {
						OR = {
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:greek
								value >= 0.50
							}
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:rhomaios
								value >= 0.50
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_AYDIN
				s:STATE_AYDIN = {
					any_scope_state = {
						OR = {
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:greek
								value >= 0.50
							}
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:rhomaios
								value >= 0.50
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 2
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = {
			name = turkfm_greek_rebellion_cooldown
			years = 2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_CRETE
				s:STATE_CRETE = {
					any_scope_state = {
						OR = {
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:greek
								value >= 0.50
							}
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:rhomaios
								value >= 0.50
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			s:STATE_CRETE = {
				random_scope_state = {
					save_scope_as = grefm_revolt_state_scope
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_ALBANIA
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_THESSALIA
				s:STATE_ALBANIA = {
					any_scope_state = {
						OR = {
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:greek
								value >= 0.50
							}
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:rhomaios
								value >= 0.50
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			s:STATE_THESSALIA = {
				random_scope_state = {
					save_scope_as = grefm_revolt_state_scope
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_ALBANIA
				s:STATE_ALBANIA = {
					any_scope_state = {
						OR = {
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:greek
								value >= 0.50
							}
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:rhomaios
								value >= 0.50
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			s:STATE_ALBANIA = {
				random_scope_state = {
					save_scope_as = grefm_revolt_state_scope
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_MACEDONIA
				s:STATE_MACEDONIA = {
					any_scope_state = {
						OR = {
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:greek
								value >= 0.50
							}
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:rhomaios
								value >= 0.50
							}
						}
						
					}
				}
			}
			s:STATE_MACEDONIA = {
				random_scope_state = {
					save_scope_as = grefm_revolt_state_scope
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_AYDIN
				s:STATE_AYDIN = {
					any_scope_state = {
						OR = {
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:greek
								value >= 0.50
							}
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:rhomaios
								value >= 0.50
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			s:STATE_AYDIN = {
				random_scope_state = {
					save_scope_as = grefm_revolt_state_scope
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_CYPRUS
				s:STATE_CYPRUS = {
					any_scope_state = {
						OR = {
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:greek
								value >= 0.50
							}
							radical_fraction = {
								culture = cu:rhomaios
								value >= 0.50
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			s:STATE_CYPRUS = {
				random_scope_state = {
					save_scope_as = grefm_revolt_state_scope
				}
			}
		}
		turkfm_hellenic_revolt_effect = yes
		scope:turkfm_greek_revolt_scope = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.296 # The Birth of the X State
			}
			remove_variable = turkfm_greek_rebellion_tracker
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Bring them to Heel
		name = turkfm.290.a
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				turkfm_can_escalate_tension_trigger = yes
			}
			turkfm_add_large_escalation_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:turkfm_greek_revolt_scope = {
				make_independent = yes
			}
		}
		create_diplomatic_play = {
			name = turkfm_greek_rebellion
			target_country = scope:turkfm_greek_revolt_scope
			type = dp_annex_war
			target_state = scope:turkfm_greek_revolt_capital_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Grant Autonomy
		name = turkfm.290.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				turkfm_can_escalate_tension_trigger = yes
			}
			turkfm_add_medium_escalation_effect = yes
		}
		scope:turkfm_greek_revolt_scope = {
			increase_autonomy = yes
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_autonomy_granted
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_imperial_weakness
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.309 = { # Adds the Eastern Question JE
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_global_variable = turkfm_separatism_complete
			has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
			has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_separatism_main
		}
		c:TUR ?= {
			has_diplomatic_relevance = root
			any_scope_state = {
				region = sr:region_balkans
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_eqfm_started
			}
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_turkfm_eastern_question
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_turkfm_eastern_question
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.300 # The Eastern Question
			}
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.310 = { # Brigands Raid Turkish Lands 
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_brigandage_event_scope
	
	title = turkfm.310.t
	desc = turkfm.310.d
	flavor = turkfm.310.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "rp1_social_banditry"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm.229
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_journal_entry = je_balkfm_brigandage
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = turkfm_brigandage_event_var
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_brigandage_event_scope
				remove_variable = turkfm_brigandage_event_var
			}
		}
		set_global_variable = {
			name = turkfm_global_reference_var
			value = money_amount_multiplier_small
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Offer Compensation
		name = turkfm.310.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_brigandage_reparations_negative
			months = normal_modifier_time
			multiplier = global_var:turkfm_global_reference_var
		}
		c:TUR = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_brigandage_reparations_positive
				months = normal_modifier_time
				multiplier = global_var:turkfm_global_reference_var
			}
			post_notification = notification_turkfm_brigandage_reparations
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = 15
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ignore the Complaint
		name = turkfm.310.b
		c:TUR = {
			post_notification = notification_turkfm_brigandage_permitted
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = -15
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		remove_global_variable = turkfm_global_reference_var
	}
	
}

			}

	option = { # Halt Support
		name = turkfm.311.a
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_supporting_gunrunners
			}
			remove_modifier = modifier_turkfm_supporting_gunrunners
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = modifier_balkfm_ottoman_gunrunners
			}
			remove_modifier = modifier_balkfm_ottoman_gunrunners
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm_ottoman_gunrunners_effect2
			set_variable = {
				name = balkfm_ottoman_gunrunners_lockout
				years = 2
			}
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = 15
		}
		c:TUR = {
			post_notification = notification_turkfm_gunrunners_halted
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Continue Support
		name = turkfm.311.b
		create_incident = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = 10
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = 15
		}
		c:TUR = {
			post_notification = notification_turkfm_gunrunners_continued
		}
	}
}

turkfm.320 = { # A Crisis in Rumelia <- Sets Variables and Starts Warmup Chain
	type = country_event
	placement = root

	desc = turkfm.310.d
	flavor = turkfm.310.f

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm_check_phase_effect during transition to crisis phase
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_variable = turkfm_separatism_phase_var
			}
			global_var:turkfm_separatism_phase_var != 5 # Crisis
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_initialize_crisis_effect = yes
		every_country = {	
			limit = {
				has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_eastern_question
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.321 # A Crisis in Rumelia (Notify Country of Crisis)
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.310.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = turkfm_no_effects
	}

}

turkfm.322 = { # Rebel Country Takes Up Arms!
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.322.t
	desc = turkfm.322.d
	flavor = turkfm.322.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_springtime_of_nations"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_variable = turkfm_crisis_var
		global_var:turkfm_crisis_var >= 30
		any_scope_state = {
			has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_race_riots
		}
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_variable = turkfm_separatism_phase_var
			}
			global_var:turkfm_separatism_phase_var != 5 # Crisis
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		months = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_create_rebellion_effect = yes
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_rebellion_tag_tracker
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_rebellion_scope
		}
		scope:turkfm_rebellion_scope = {
			remove_variable = turkfm_rebellion_tag_tracker
			set_variable = turkfm_crisis_attacker
			set_variable = turkfm_crisis_upstart
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_relevance = root
			}
			create_bidirectional_truce = {
				country = scope:turkfm_rebellion_scope
				months = 60
			}
		}
		create_bidirectional_truce = {
			country = scope:turkfm_rebellion_scope
			months = 60
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.322.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = turkfm_crisis_rebellion_tt
	}

}

turkfm.323 = { # Subject Country Rebels!
	orphan = yes
}

turkfm.324 = { # A Chance at Deconfliction (Third Party Event)
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:ottoman_scope
	
	title = turkfm.324.t
	desc = turkfm.324.d
	flavor = turkfm.324.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "ep1_clandestine_meeting"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_variable = turkfm_crisis_var
		country_rank >= rank_value:great_power
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = turkfm_deconfliction_var
		}
		global_var:turkfm_crisis_var >= 30
		global_var:turkfm_crisis_var < 90
		turkfm_crisis_deconfliction_trigger = yes
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOR = {
			global_var:turkfm_separatism_phase_var != 5 # Crisis
			has_global_variable = turkfm_separatism_phase_var
			has_variable = turkfm_crisis_attacker
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 2
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Attempt Deconfliction
		name = turkfm.324.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = turkfm.324.a.tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:GBR ?= this
			}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = turkfm_deconfliction_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				c:FRA ?= this
			}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = turkfm_deconfliction_var
				value = 2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				c:RUS ?= this
			}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = turkfm_deconfliction_var
				value = 3
			}
		}
		c:TUR = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.325 # A Chance at Deconfliction (Ottoman Event)
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Continue into the Fight
		name = turkfm.324.b
		custom_tooltip = turkfm.324.b.tt
	}

}

turkfm.325 = { # A Chance at Deconfliction (Ottoman Event)
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_deconfliction_scope
	
	title = turkfm.325.t
	desc = turkfm.325.d
	flavor = turkfm.325.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "ep1_clandestine_meeting"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm.324
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = turkfm_deconfliction_var
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:turkfm_deconfliction_var = 1
			}
			c:GBR ?= {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_deconfliction_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:turkfm_deconfliction_var = 2
			}
			c:FRA ?= {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_deconfliction_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:turkfm_deconfliction_var = 3
			}
			c:RUS ?= {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_deconfliction_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.325.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_crisis_deconfliction_tt
			scope:turkfm_deconfliction_scope = {
				remove_variable = turkfm_crisis_attacker
				set_variable = turkfm_crisis_deconflicted
			}
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:turkfm_deconfliction_scope
			value = 15
		}
		remove_global_variable = turkfm_deconfliction_var
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.325.b
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:turkfm_deconfliction_scope
			value = -15
		}
		remove_global_variable = turkfm_deconfliction_var
	}

}

turkfm.326 = { # Balkan Crisis Superevent <- Creates DP
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.326.t
	desc = turkfm.326.d
	flavor = turkfm.326.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "turkfm_balkan_crisis"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ottoman.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_variable = turkfm_crisis_var
		global_var:turkfm_crisis_var >= 100
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_country = {	
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_crisis_leader
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_truce_with = c:TUR
				}
				end_truce = c:TUR
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_crisis_leader_scope
		}
		scope:turkfm_crisis_leader_scope = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				type = dp_turkfm_crisis
				target_country = c:TUR
				war = yes
			}
		}
		remove_global_variable = turkfm_crisis_var
		remove_global_variable = turkfm_crisis_progress_var
		set_global_variable = turkfm_crisis_launched
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = turkfm_crisis_attacker
					has_variable = turkfm_crisis_defender
				}
				has_truce_with = c:TUR
			}
			end_truce = c:TUR
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.327 # Balkan Crisis Superevent <- Participant Event
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.326.a
		default_option = yes
	}

}

turkfm.327 = { # Balkan Crisis Superevent <- Participant Event
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.327.t
	desc = turkfm.327.d
	flavor = turkfm.327.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "turkfm_balkan_crisis"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ottoman.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm.326
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_diplomatic_play = {
			limit = {
				is_diplomatic_play_type = dp_turkfm_crisis
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_crisis_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_crisis_attacker
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_crisis_leader
				}
			}
			scope:turkfm_crisis_scope = {
				add_initiator_backers = { root }
				add_diplomatic_play_war_support  = {
					target = root
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_crisis_defender
			}
			scope:turkfm_crisis_scope = {
				add_target_backers = { root }
				add_diplomatic_play_war_support = {
					target = root
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.327.a
		default_option = yes
	}

}

		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_no_effects
			turkfm_cleanup_congress_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { # For Deconflicted/Non-Participants
		name = turkfm.328.c
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				c:TUR = this
				has_variable = turkfm_crisis_attacker
				has_variable = turkfm_crisis_defender
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_no_effects

		}
	}

#### INTERNATIONAL CONGRESS EVENTS ####

turkfm.330 = { # Congress System Monitor
	type = country_event
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_variable = turkfm_congress_var
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = turkfm_congress_cooldown_var
		}
		any_country = {
			OR = {
				has_variable = turkfm_crisis_attacker
				has_variable = turkfm_crisis_deconflicted
			}
		}
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_international_congress
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_congress_issue_var
			}
			remove_variable = turkfm_congress_issue_var
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = turkfm_crisis_attacker
					has_variable = turkfm_crisis_deconflicted
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_congress_issue_scope
			set_variable = turkfm_congress_issue_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {	
				exists = scope:turkfm_congress_issue_scope
			}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = turkfm_congress_cooldown_var
				days = 45
			}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = turkfm_congress_vote_var
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_congress_issue_scope = {
						has_variable = turkfm_crisis_attacker
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_international_congress
					}
					trigger_event = {
						id = turkfm.332 # The Issue of X
					}
					trigger_event = {
						id = turkfm.338 # Resolution on the X Matter
						days = 45
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					scope:turkfm_congress_issue_scope = {
						has_variable = turkfm_crisis_deconflicted
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_international_congress
					}
					trigger_event = {
						id = turkfm.337 # The Convention of X
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_international_congress
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = turkfm.339 # The Treaty of X
				}
			}
			turkfm_force_deconfliction_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.332 = { # The Issue of X
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_congress_host_scope
	
	title = turkfm.332.t
	desc = turkfm.332.d
	flavor = turkfm.332.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_congress.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm.330
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_international_congress
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_congress_host
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_congress_host_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_congress_issue_var
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_congress_issue_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.332.a
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = c:TUR
					type = rivalry
				}
			}
		}
		highlighted_option = yes
		show_as_unavailable = {
			always = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = turkfm_congress_support_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_rank >= rank_value:great_power
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = turkfm_congress_vote_var
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = turkfm_congress_support_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					country_rank = rank_value:major_power
					country_rank = rank_value:unrecognized_major_power
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = turkfm_congress_vote_var
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = turkfm_congress_support_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_rank <= rank_value:minor_power
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = turkfm_congress_vote_var
				add = 1
			}
			custom_tooltip = turkfm_congress_support_1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.332.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = c:TUR
					type = alliance
				}
			}
		}
		highlighted_option = yes
		show_as_unavailable = {
			always = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = turkfm_congress_oppose_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_rank >= rank_value:great_power
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = turkfm_congress_vote_var
				subtract = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = turkfm_congress_oppose_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					country_rank = rank_value:major_power
					country_rank = rank_value:unrecognized_major_power
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = turkfm_congress_vote_var
				subtract = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = turkfm_congress_oppose_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_rank <= rank_value:minor_power
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = turkfm_congress_vote_var
				subtract = 1
			}
			custom_tooltip = turkfm_congress_oppose_1
		}
	}

}

		}

			custom_tooltip = turkfm_congress_issue_fail
		}
	}
	
}

	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered from GLOBAL
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
		c:MON = {
			save_scope_as = montenegro_scope
		}
		balkfm_save_ali_pasha_scopes = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:MON ?= this
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.331 # Negociations At Humac
				months = 14 # should be early 1937
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.800.a
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:MON ?= this
			}
			show_as_tooltip = {
				turkfm_karadag_regress_effect = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				c:TUR ?= this
			}
			turkfm_karadag_advance_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.801 = { # Negociations on Headtaking (TUR)
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:montenegro_scope
	
	title = turkfm.801.t
	desc = turkfm.801.d
	flavor = turkfm.801.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "asia_politician_parliament_motion"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm_renounce_headtaking_button
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c:MON = {
			save_scope_as = montenegro_scope
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # For TUR, reject headtaking offer
		name = turkfm.801.a
		default_option = yes
		turkfm_add_small_escalation_effect = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_retained_headtaking
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		c:MON = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.802 # Negociations On Headtaking
			}
			set_variable = turkfm_headtaking_rejected
		}
	}
	
	option = { # For TUR, accept headtaking offer
		name = turkfm.801.b
		turkfm_add_medium_deescalation_effect = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_abolished_headtaking
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		c:MON = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.802 # Negociations On Headtaking
			}
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.802 = { # Negociations on Headtaking (MON)
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.802.t
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = turkfm.802.d1
			trigger = {
				has_variable = turkfm_headtaking_rejected
			}
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = turkfm.802.d2
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_headtaking_rejected
				}
			}
		}
	}
	flavor = turkfm.802.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_2char_discussion

	left_icon = scope:turkfm_ruler_scope
	right_icon = scope:ottoman_ruler_scope
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm.801
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c:TUR ?= {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
			ruler = {
				save_scope_as = ottoman_ruler_scope
			}
		}
		ruler = {
			save_scope_as = turkfm_ruler_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # For MON, headtaking offer rejected, retain headtaking
		name = turkfm.802.a
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			has_variable = turkfm_headtaking_rejected
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_retained_headtaking
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
	}
	
	option = { # For MON, headtaking offer rejected, abolish unilaterally
		name = turkfm.802.b
		trigger = {
			has_variable = turkfm_headtaking_rejected
		}
		remove_modifier = modifier_turkfm_practicing_headtaking
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_unilaterally_abolished_headtaking
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
	}
	
	option = { # For MON, headtaking offer accepted
		name = turkfm.802.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = turkfm_headtaking_rejected
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = modifier_turkfm_practicing_headtaking
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_abolished_headtaking
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		remove_variable = turkfm_headtaking_rejected
	}

}

			}
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.804 = { # Montenegrin Lands Gained
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.804.t
	desc = turkfm.804.d
	flavor = turkfm.804.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_gold_prospectors"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		trigger_if = {
			limit = {
				c:TUR ?= this
			}
			global_var:turkfm_karadag_var <= 0
		}
		trigger_else_if = {
			limit = {
				c:MON ?= this
			}
			global_var:turkfm_karadag_var >= 500
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_next_province_effect = yes
		turkfm_claim_province_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:TUR ?= this
			}
			c:MON ?= {
				trigger_event = {
					id = turkfm.805 # Montenegrin Lands Lost
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				c:MON ?= this
			}
			c:TUR ?= {
				trigger_event = {
					id = turkfm.805 # Montenegrin Lands Lost
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.804.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_province_gained
			turkfm_next_province_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
}

#### BORDER CONFLICT MECHANICAL EVENTS

turkfm.810 = { # Reclaiming the Hinterlands
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.810.t
	desc = turkfm.810.d
	flavor = turkfm.810.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "africa_construction_colony"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_military.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm_border_raid_button
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_karadag
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_busy = no
				has_role = general
				is_ruler = no
			}
			save_scope_as = expedition_leader_1
		}
		if = {
			random_scope_character = {
				limit = {
					is_busy = no
					is_ruler = no
					has_role = general
					OR = {
						has_trait = surveyor
						has_trait = mountain_commander
						has_trait = basic_offensive_planner
						has_trait = experienced_offensive_planner
						has_trait = expert_offensive_planner
					}
					NOT = {
						scope:expedition_leader_1 ?= this
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = expedition_leader_2
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_scope_character = {
				limit = {
					is_busy = no
					is_ruler = no
					has_role = general
					NOT = {
						scope:expedition_leader_1 ?= this
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = expedition_leader_2
			}
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_busy = no
				is_ruler = no
				has_role = general
				NOR = {
					scope:expedition_leader_1 ?= this
					scope:expedition_leader_2 ?= this
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = expedition_leader_3
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_busy = no
				is_ruler = no
				has_role = general
				NOR = {
					scope:expedition_leader_1 ?= this
					scope:expedition_leader_2 ?= this
					scope:expedition_leader_3 ?= this
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = expedition_leader_4
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.810.a
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:expedition_leader_1
		}
		scope:expedition_leader_1 ?= {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_leading_expedition
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.810.b
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:expedition_leader_2
		}
		scope:expedition_leader_2 ?= {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_leading_expedition
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.810.c
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:expedition_leader_3
		}
		scope:expedition_leader_3 ?= {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_leading_expedition
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.810.e
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:expedition_leader_4
		}
		scope:expedition_leader_4 ?= {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_leading_expedition
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = turkfm.811 # Raiding Party Arrives in the Hinterlands
			days = { 15 45 }
		}
		set_variable = turkfm_expedition_transit_var
	}
	
}

turkfm.814 = { # The Gaols of Centinje
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.814.t
	desc = turkfm.814.d
	flavor = turkfm.814.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_prison"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_scales.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm_visit_gaol_button
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_template = template_balkfm_captive_bosnian
					has_template = template_balkfm_captive_albanian
					has_template = template_balkfm_captive_serbian
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_captive_1_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = scope:turkfm_captive_1_scope
			}
			random_character_in_void = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_template = template_balkfm_captive_bosnian
						has_template = template_balkfm_captive_albanian
						has_template = template_balkfm_captive_serbian
					}
					scope:turkfm_captive_1_scope != this
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_captive_2_scope
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:turkfm_captive_2_scope
				}
				random_character_in_void = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_template = template_balkfm_captive_bosnian
							has_template = template_balkfm_captive_albanian
							has_template = template_balkfm_captive_serbian
						}
						scope:turkfm_captive_1_scope != this
						scope:turkfm_captive_2_scope != this
					}
					save_scope_as = turkfm_captive_3_scope
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						exists = scope:turkfm_captive_3_scope
					}
					random_character_in_void = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_template = template_balkfm_captive_bosnian
								has_template = template_balkfm_captive_albanian
								has_template = template_balkfm_captive_serbian
							}
							scope:turkfm_captive_1_scope != this
							scope:turkfm_captive_2_scope != this
							scope:turkfm_captive_3_scope != this
						}
						save_scope_as = turkfm_captive_4_scope
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.814.1
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:turkfm_captive_1_scope
		}
		scope:turkfm_captive_1_scope = {
			set_variable = turkfm_captive_event_target
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.814.2
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:turkfm_captive_2_scope
		}
		scope:turkfm_captive_2_scope = {
			set_variable = turkfm_captive_event_target
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.814.3
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:turkfm_captive_3_scope
		}
		scope:turkfm_captive_3_scope = {
			set_variable = turkfm_captive_event_target
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.814.4
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:turkfm_captive_4_scope
		}
		scope:turkfm_captive_4_scope = {
			set_variable = turkfm_captive_event_target
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.814.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_nothing_happens
			remove_variable = turkfm_ransom_var
		}
	}
	
}

			save_scope_as = turkfm_captive_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Post Bail
		name = turkfm.815.a

			strata = poor

			value = small_radicals
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_accepted_ransom
			months = short_modifier_time
		}
		c:MON = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.816 # Ottoman Noble Ransom Event
				days = { 7 14 }
			}
			set_variable = turkfm_ransom_accepted
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 8
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Uhh, not our problem
		name = turkfm.815.b
		add_radicals = {
			strata = rich
			culture = cu:turkish
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_refused_ransom
			months = short_modifier_time

		}
		c:MON = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.816 # Ottoman Noble Ransom Event
				days = { 7 14 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.816 = { # Ottoman Reply to Ransom
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = {

			trigger = {
				has_variable = turkfm_ransom_accepted
			}
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = turkfm.816.t2
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_ransom_accepted
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = turkfm.816.d1
			trigger = {
				has_variable = turkfm_ransom_accepted
			}
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = turkfm.816.d2
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_ransom_accepted
				}
			}
		}
	}
	flavor = turkfm.816.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:turkfm_captive_scope
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm.815
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_captive_event_target
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_captive_scope
		}
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {	# Ransom Accepted
		name = turkfm.816.b
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			has_variable = turkfm_ransom_accepted
		}
		scope:turkfm_captive_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_ransomed_noble
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		remove_variable = turkfm_ransom_accepted
	}
	
	option = { # Accept the News
		name = turkfm.816.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = turkfm_ransom_accepted
			}
		}
		scope:turkfm_captive_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_rejected_hostage
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_ransom_failed
			months = short_modifier_time
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Cool story bro, where's my sword
		name = turkfm.816.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = turkfm_ransom_accepted
			}
		}
		show_as_tooltip = {
			scope:turkfm_captive_scope = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
		}
		create_incident = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = 10 # this is higher because you're just being vindictive here
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_executed_noble
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		c:TUR = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.817 # Ottoman Noble Beheaded
				days = { 5 15 }
			}
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.834 = { # Ottoman Noble Captured
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.834.t
	desc = turkfm.834.d
	flavor = turkfm.834.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_2char_discussion
	
	left_icon = scope:turkfm_expedition_leader_scope
	right_icon = scope:turkfm_captive_scope
	
	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gbbf_backgrounds/gbbf_mountain_road.dds"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_military.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/DLC/1.3_ip1/Events/unspecific/gunboat_diplomacy"
	
	duration = 1
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		has_variable = turkfm_village_skirmish_var
		turkfm_captured_nobles_value < 3
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_karadag
			has_variable = turkfm_village_skirmish_var
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 2
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = turkfm_expedition_cooldown_var
			days = 10
		}
		turkfm_karadag_scopes_effect = yes
		turkfm_generate_captive_effect = yes
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_captive_var
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_captive_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Let Them Go
		name = turkfm.834.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_captive_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
		}
		c:TUR = {
			post_notification = notification_turkfm_noble_released
		}
		add_radicals = {
			value = small_radicals
		}
		turkfm_add_small_peril_effect = yes
		turkfm_karadag_regress_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Lock them up
		name = turkfm.834.b
		scope:turkfm_captive_scope = {
			remove_variable = turkfm_captive_var
		}
		create_incident = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = 5
		}
		c:TUR = {
			post_notification = notification_turkfm_noble_captured
		}
		turkfm_karadag_advance_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Off With Their Head!
		name = turkfm.834.c
		scope:turkfm_captive_scope = {
			remove_variable = turkfm_captive_var
			set_variable = turkfm_captive_event_target
		}
		show_as_tooltip = {
			scope:turkfm_captive_scope = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
		}
		create_incident = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = 10
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_executed_noble
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		c:TUR = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.817 # Ottoman Noble Beheaded
				days = { 5 15 }
			}
		}
		turkfm_karadag_advance_effect = yes
		turkfm_add_medium_progress_effect = yes
		turkfm_add_small_peril_effect = yes
	}
	
}

turkfm.900 = { # The Pirates of the Adriatic

	}

		turkfm_jack_sparrow_effect = yes
		set_variable = turkfm_piracy_started
	}

		name = turkfm.900.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = turkfm.900.tt
	}

turkfm.901 = { # Pacifying the Adriatic
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.901.t
	desc = turkfm.901.d
	flavor = turkfm.901.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "africa_construction_colony"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_piracy.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm_deploy_expedition_button
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = turkfm_jack_sparrow_whacked
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_busy = no
				has_role = admiral
				is_ruler = no
			}
			save_scope_as = expedition_leader_1
		}
		if = {
			random_scope_character = {
				limit = {
					is_busy = no
					is_ruler = no
					has_role = admiral
					OR = {
						has_trait = basic_naval_commander
						has_trait = experienced_naval_commander
						has_trait = expert_naval_commander
						has_trait = convoy_raider_commander
						has_trait = experienced_convoy_raider
						has_trait = expert_convoy_raider
					}
					NOT = {
						scope:expedition_leader_1 ?= this
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = expedition_leader_2
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_scope_character = {
				limit = {
					is_busy = no
					is_ruler = no
					has_role = admiral
					NOT = {
						scope:expedition_leader_1 ?= this
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = expedition_leader_2
			}
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_busy = no
				is_ruler = no
				has_role = admiral
				NOR = {
					scope:expedition_leader_1 ?= this
					scope:expedition_leader_2 ?= this
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = expedition_leader_3
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_busy = no
				is_ruler = no
				has_role = admiral
				NOR = {
					scope:expedition_leader_1 ?= this
					scope:expedition_leader_2 ?= this
					scope:expedition_leader_3 ?= this
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = expedition_leader_4
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.901.a
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:expedition_leader_1
		}
		scope:expedition_leader_1 ?= {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_leading_expedition
		}
		turkfm_jack_sparrow_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.901.b
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:expedition_leader_2
		}
		scope:expedition_leader_2 ?= {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_leading_expedition
		}
		turkfm_jack_sparrow_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.901.c
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:expedition_leader_3
		}
		scope:expedition_leader_3 ?= {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_leading_expedition
		}
		turkfm_jack_sparrow_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.901.e
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:expedition_leader_4
		}
		scope:expedition_leader_4 ?= {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_leading_expedition
		}
		turkfm_jack_sparrow_effect = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = turkfm.902 # Cutler Beckett Arrives in the Adriatic
			days = { 15 45 }
		}
		set_variable = turkfm_expedition_transit_var
	}

}

	left_icon = scope:turkfm_cutler_beckett_scope
	
	event_image = {

	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_piracy.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/DLC/1.3_ip1/Events/unspecific/gunboat_diplomacy"
	
	duration = 2

turkfm.905 = { # Treating with Corsairs
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.905.t
	desc = turkfm.905.d
	flavor = turkfm.905.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_gunboat_diplomacy"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_piracy.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm_hire_retired_pirates_button
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_pirates_of_the_adriatic
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_is_adriatic = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_piracy_state_scope
		}
		create_character = {
			template = template_turkfm_hector_barbossa
			on_created = {
				place_character_in_void = 12
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_turkfm_hector_barbossa
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_hector_barbossa_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.905.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_hired_pirates
			months = long_modifier_time
			is_decaying = yes
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_corsair_recruits
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.905.b
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_hector_barbossa_scope = {
			hidden_effect = {
				free_character_from_void = yes
			}
			add_character_role = admiral
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_hired_pirates
			months = long_modifier_time
			is_decaying = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.905.c
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_nothing_happens
			scope:turkfm_hector_barbossa_scope = {
				hidden_effect = {
					free_character_from_void = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		remove_variable = turkfm_selecting_recruits
	}

}

turkfm.908 = { # Jack Sparrow Clapped in Irons!
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.908.t
	desc = turkfm.908.d
	flavor = turkfm.908.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_2char_adventure
	
	left_icon = scope:turkfm_cutler_beckett_scope
	right_icon = scope:turkfm_jack_sparrow_scope
	
	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/gbbf_backgrounds/gbbf_open_ocean.dds"
	}
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_hostile_court"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_piracy.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm.907 via turkfm_complete_piracy_expedition_effect
	}
	
	immediate = {
		turkfm_piracy_scopes_effect = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_pirates_of_the_adriatic
				NOT = {
					has_variable = turkfm_jack_sparrow_captor
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.909 # Jack Sparrow Whacked
			}
		}
		remove_variable = turkfm_jack_sparrow_captor
		set_global_variable = turkfm_jack_sparrow_whacked
	}
	
	option = { # Throw Him in Jail
		name = turkfm.908.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_pacified_adriatic
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		scope:turkfm_jack_sparrow_scope = {
			custom_tooltip = turkfm_thrown_in_jail_tt
		}
		turkfm_advance_ottomanism1_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # To the Gallows
		name = turkfm.908.b
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_pacified_adriatic
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		scope:turkfm_jack_sparrow_scope = {
			show_as_tooltip = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
		}
		turkfm_advance_ottomanism1_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Give Him a Job
		name = turkfm.908.c
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_pacified_adriatic
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		scope:turkfm_jack_sparrow_scope = {
			add_character_role = admiral
			hidden_effect = {
				free_character_from_void = yes
			}
			remove_trait = reckless
			add_trait = trait_turkfm_corsair
		}
		add_radicals = {
			pop_type = officers
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_hired_pirates
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_hired_pirates
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		turkfm_advance_ottomanism1_effect = yes
	}

}

#### PIRATES OF THE ADRIATIC PIRACY EVENTS ####

turkfm.910 = { # Coastal Village Raided!
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_piracy_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.910.t
	desc = turkfm.910.d
	flavor = turkfm.910.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "southamerica_war_civilians"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_piracy.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 2
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = turkfm_expedition_cooldown_var
		}
		OR = {
			turkfm_has_adriatic_expedition_trigger = yes
			any_scope_state = {
				state_is_adriatic = yes
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_coasts_raided
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = turkfm_jack_sparrow_whacked
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = turkfm_expedition_cooldown_var
			days = 45
		}
		turkfm_piracy_scopes_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				turkfm_has_adriatic_expedition_trigger = yes
			}
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					state_is_adriatic = yes
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_coasts_raided
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_piracy_state_scope
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					state_is_adriatic = yes
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_coasts_raided
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_piracy_state_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Maybe they shouldn't live on the coast
		name = turkfm.910.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_piracy_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_coasts_raided
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata = poor
				value = small_radicals
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Provide Relief
		name = turkfm.910.b
		scope:turkfm_piracy_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_coasts_raided
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_aid_distributed_state
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				strata = poor
				value = small_radicals
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_turkfm_aid_distributed_country
			months = short_modifier_time
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Distribute expedition supplies
		name = turkfm.910.c
		highlighted_option = yes
		trigger = {
			turkfm_has_adriatic_expedition_trigger = yes
		}
		scope:turkfm_piracy_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_coasts_raided
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_aid_distributed_state
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_large_peril_effect = yes
		turkfm_add_medium_progress_effect = yes
	}
	
}

		turkfm_remove_small_progress_effect = yes
	}

}

turkfm.915 = { # Slavers Intercepted
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.915.t
	desc = turkfm.915.d
	flavor = turkfm.915.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_gunboat_diplomacy"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_piracy.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 2
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = turkfm_expedition_cooldown_var
		}
		c:TUR ?= {
			NOT = {
				has_law = law_type:law_slavery_banned
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_pirates_of_the_adriatic
			NOR = {
				c:TUR ?= this 
				has_law = law_type:law_slavery_banned
			}
			any_trade_route = {
				OR = {
					exporter.owner = C:TUR
					importer.owner = c:TUR
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = turkfm_jack_sparrow_whacked
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 5
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = turkfm_expedition_cooldown_var
			days = 45
		}
		turkfm_piracy_scopes_effect = yes
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_pirates_of_the_adriatic
				NOR = {
					c:TUR ?= this 
					has_law = law_type:law_slavery_banned
				}
				any_trade_route = {
					OR = {
						exporter.owner = C:TUR
						importer.owner = c:TUR
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_piracy_country_scope
			random_primary_culture = {
				save_scope_as = turkfm_piracy_culture_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Arrest the Slavers
		name = turkfm.915.a
		default_option = yes
		change_relations = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = -15
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:turkfm_piracy_country_scope
			value = -15
		}
		create_diplomatic_catalyst = {
			type = catalyst_diplomatic_incident
			target = c:TUR
		}
		create_diplomatic_catalyst = {
			type = catalyst_diplomatic_incident
			target = scope:turkfm_piracy_country_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.915.b
		change_relations = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = 20
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:turkfm_piracy_country_scope
			value = 20
		}
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				law_stance = {
					law = law_type:law_slavery_banned
					value > 0
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_tolerated_slavers
				months = normal_modifier_time
				is_decaying = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Shelter the Slaves
		name = turkfm.915.c
		trigger = {
			has_law = law_type:law_slavery_banned
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = -30
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:turkfm_piracy_country_scope
			value = -30
		}
		create_diplomatic_catalyst = {
			type = catalyst_diplomatic_incident
			target = c:TUR
		}
		create_diplomatic_catalyst = {
			type = catalyst_diplomatic_incident
			target = scope:turkfm_piracy_country_scope
		}
	}

}

turkfm.919 = { # Adds the Piracy JE
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_global_variable = turkfm_jack_sparrow_whacked
			has_journal_entry = je_turkfm_pirates_of_the_adriatic
		}
		OR = {
			any_scope_state = {
				state_is_adriatic = yes
				is_coastal = yes
			}
			AND = {
				c:TUR ?= {
					any_scope_state = {
						state_is_adriatic = yes
						is_coastal = yes
					}
				}
				any_trade_route = {
					OR = {
						exporter.owner = c:TUR
						importer.owner = c:TUR
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = turkfm_piracy_started
			}
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_turkfm_pirates_of_the_adriatic
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = turkfm_piracy_started
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_turkfm_pirates_of_the_adriatic
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = turkfm.900 # The Pirates of the Adriatic
			}
		}
	}
	
}

		}
		turkfm_piracy_scopes_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Slow Down
		name = turkfm.931.a
		default_option = yes
		turkfm_remove_small_progress_effect = yes
		turkfm_add_small_peril_effect = yes
		add_loyalists = {
			pop_type = soldiers
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		add_radicals = {
			pop_type = officers
			value = medium_radicals
		}
	}

		turkfm_add_medium_peril_effect = yes
		add_radicals = {
			pop_type = soldiers
			value = medium_radicals
		}

			pop_type = officers
			value = medium_radicals
		}
	}

turkfm.938 = { # Beckett & Sparrow Duel
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.938.t
	desc = turkfm.938.d
	flavor = turkfm.938.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_highlander
	
	left_icon = scope:turkfm_cutler_beckett_scope
	right_icon = scope:turkfm_jack_sparrow_scope
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_naval_battle"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_piracy.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 2
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		has_variable = turkfm_piracy_chase_var
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = turkfm_maelstrom_var
		}
		var:turkfm_expedition_progress_var >= 5
		global_var:turkfm_pirates_var >= 3
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = turkfm_jack_sparrow_whacked
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = turkfm_expedition_cooldown_var
			days = 90
		}
		set_global_variable = {
			name = turkfm_maelstrom_var
			value = 0
		}
		turkfm_piracy_scopes_effect = yes
		remove_variable = turkfm_piracy_chase_var
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.938.a
		default_option = yes
		trigger_event = {
			id = turkfm.939 # Naval Duel Outcome
		}
		random_list = {
			5 = {
				set_global_variable = {
					name = turkfm_maelstrom_var
					value = 1 # Jack Wins
				}
				set_global_variable = {
					name = turkfm_maelstrom_var
					value = 2 # Cutler Wins
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.938.b
		turkfm_remove_large_progress_effect = yes
		turkfm_add_small_peril_effect = yes
	}

}

turkfm.939 = { # Naval Duel Outcome
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.939.t
	desc = turkfm.939.d
	flavor = turkfm.939.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_naval_battle"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_piracy.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 2
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by turkfm.938
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = turkfm_jack_sparrow_whacked
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = turkfm_expedition_cooldown_var
			days = 45
		}
		turkfm_jack_sparrow_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:turkfm_maelstrom_var = 1 # Jack Wins
			}
			random_character_in_void = {
				limit = {
					has_template = template_turkfm_jack_sparrow
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_duel_victor_scope
			}
			random_scope_character = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_leading_expedition
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_duel_loser_scope
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_character_in_void = {
				limit = {
					has_template = template_turkfm_jack_sparrow
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_duel_loser_scope
			}
			random_scope_character = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_leading_expedition
				}
				save_scope_as = turkfm_duel_victor_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Jack Wins
		name = turkfm.939.a
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			global_var:turkfm_maelstrom_var = 1
		}
		scope:turkfm_cutler_beckett_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_lost_naval_duel
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		turkfm_remove_large_progress_effect = yes
		turkfm_add_large_peril_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Cutler Wins
		name = turkfm.939.b
		trigger = {
			global_var:turkfm_maelstrom_var = 2
		}
		scope:turkfm_cutler_beckett_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_turkfm_won_naval_duel
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		turkfm_add_large_progress_effect = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		remove_global_variable = turkfm_maelstrom_var
	}

}

	dlc = dlc_grefm

	}

		random_scope_general = {

	}

				name = turkfm_senussi_var
				subtract = 10
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				name = turkfm_senussi_var
				max = 100
				min = 0
			}
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.1114 = { # Senusiyya Takes Root in State
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_senussi_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.1114.t
	desc = turkfm.1114.d
	flavor = turkfm.1114.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_adventure
	
	left_icon = scope:turkfm_senussi_scope
	
	event_image = {
		video = "middleeast_islam"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		var:turkfm_senussi_var >= 70
		NOT = {
			has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_desert_raids
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			OR = {
				state_region = s:STATE_LIBYA
				state_region = s:STATE_LIBYAN_DESERT
				state_region = s:STATE_TRIPOLI
			}
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_senussi_stronghold
			}
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 4
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state_region = s:STATE_LIBYA
					state_region = s:STATE_LIBYAN_DESERT
					state_region = s:STATE_TRIPOLI
				}
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_senussi_stronghold
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_senussi_state_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				turkfm_is_senussi_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_senussi_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Allow them to Spread
		name = turkfm.1114.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_senussi_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_senussi_stronghold
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_senussi_lose_20
			change_variable = {
				name = turkfm_senussi_var
				subtract = 20
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Attempt to Supress Them
		name = turkfm.1114.b
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			has_technology_researched = centralization
			has_variable = turkfm_intimidated_sensussi
			authority >= 200
		}
		add_modifier = modifier_turkfm_desert_raids
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_supress_senusiyya_effect
			set_variable = {
				name = turkfm_desert_raids_var
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.1115 = { # Senusiyya Expunged from State
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:turkfm_senussi_state_scope
	
	title = turkfm.1115.t
	desc = turkfm.1115.d
	flavor = turkfm.1115.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_adventure
	
	left_icon = scope:turkfm_senussi_scope
	
	event_image = {
		video = "africa_desert_expedition"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		var:turkfm_senussi_var < 30
		has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_desert_raids
		any_scope_state = {
			OR = {
				state_region = s:STATE_LIBYA
				state_region = s:STATE_LIBYAN_DESERT
				state_region = s:STATE_TRIPOLI
			}
			has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_senussi_stronghold
			is_largest_state_in_region = yes
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 2
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state_region = s:STATE_LIBYA
					state_region = s:STATE_LIBYAN_DESERT
					state_region = s:STATE_TRIPOLI
				}
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_senussi_stronghold
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_senussi_state_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				turkfm_is_senussi_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = turkfm_senussi_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.1115.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:turkfm_senussi_state_scope = {
			remove_modifier = modifier_turkfm_senussi_stronghold
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = turkfm_senussi_gain_20
			change_variable = {
				name = turkfm_senussi_var
				add = 20
			}
		}
	}
	
}

turkfm.1201 = { # An Amibitious Bey
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = turkfm.1201.t
	desc = turkfm.1201.d
	flavor = turkfm.1201.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_monarch_holding_court"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		ruler = {
			has_template = template_turkfm_husaini_mustafa
		}
		year >= 1837
		exists = heir
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NAND = {
			ruler = {
				has_template = template_turkfm_husaini_mustafa
			}
			exists = heir
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		heir = {
			save_scope_as = turkfm_ahmad_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = turkfm.1201.a
		default_option = yes
		ruler = {
			kill_character = yes
		}
		heir = {
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
	}
	
}

		}
	}
